select u.n_name, '	', m.date, '	', m.text, '
' from global_message m join users u on m.id_from = u.id where m.status = 1;
SELECT f.n_name_from as n_name_from, '	', t.n_name_to as n_name_to, '	', m.date as date, '	', m.text as text, '
' FROM message m INNER JOIN mess_name_from f ON m.id = f.id INNER JOIN mess_name_to t ON m.id = t.id where n_name_from = 'admin' or n_name_to = 'admin' ORDER BY m.date

SELECT f.n_name_from as n_name_from, '	', t.n_name_to as n_name_to, '	', m.date as date, '	', m.text as text, '
' FROM message m INNER JOIN mess_name_from f ON m.id = f.id INNER JOIN mess_name_to t ON m.id = t.id where n_name_from = 'admin' or n_name_to = 'admin' ORDER BY m.date

SELECT f.n_name_from as n_name_from, '	', t.n_name_to as n_name_to, '	', m.date as date, '	', m.text as text, '
' FROM message m INNER JOIN mess_name_from f ON m.id = f.id INNER JOIN mess_name_to t ON m.id = t.id where n_name_from = 'admin' or n_name_to = 'admin' ORDER BY m.date

SELECT f.n_name_from as n_name_from, '	', t.n_name_to as n_name_to, '	', m.date as date, '	', m.text as text, '
' FROM message m INNER JOIN mess_name_from f ON m.id = f.id INNER JOIN mess_name_to t ON m.id = t.id where n_name_from = 'admin' or n_name_to = 'admin' ORDER BY m.date

SELECT f.n_name_from as n_name_from, '	', t.n_name_to as n_name_to, '	', m.date as date, '	', m.text as text, '
' FROM message m INNER JOIN mess_name_from f ON m.id = f.id INNER JOIN mess_name_to t ON m.id = t.id where n_name_from = 'admin' or n_name_to = 'admin' ORDER BY m.date

' FROM message m INNER JOIN mess_name_from f ON m.id = f.id INNER JOIN mess_name_to t ON m.id = t.id where n_name_from = 'admin' or n_name_to = 'admin' ORDER BY m.date
